/* Showing results for airports.xls */

/* CREATE TABLE */
CREATE TABLE worldairports(
City_Name VARCHAR(100),
Airport_Name VARCHAR(100),
Country VARCHAR(100),
Length_ft DOUBLE,
Elevation_ft DOUBLE,
column_5 VARCHAR(100),
Geographic_Location VARCHAR(100)
);
